[30;1m174 | [0m[35mat most the number of bytes specified. So you can try reading one byte at a[0m
[30;1m175 | [0m[35mtime till you encounter a time out. When that happens most likely the last[0m
[30;1m176 | [0m[35mcharacter you read is the termination character. Here is a quick example:[0m
[30;1m177 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m93 | [0m[35mThe programming of measurement instruments can be real pain. There are many[0m
[30;1m94 | [0m[35mdifferent protocols, sent over many different interfaces and bus systems[0m
[30;1m95 | [0m[35m(GPIB, RS232, USB). For every programming language you want to use, you have to[0m
[30;1m96 | [0m[35mfind libraries that support both your device and its bus system.[0m
[30;1m97 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m98 | [0m[35mIn order to ease this unfortunate situation, the Virtual Instrument Software[0m
[30;1m99 | [0m[35mArchitecture (VISA_) specification was defined in the middle of the 90's. Today[0m
